# Doing: Clem Feedback E2E

## Execution Mode

- **pending**: Explicit human approval before each unit; not selected.
- **spawn**: Use a sub-agent for an isolated unit.
- **direct**: Execute sequentially in this session; selected. The explicit reviewer matrix in `Execution` applies.

Every red/green unit below follows the Round110 immutable-evidence protocol. A red command writes only its named red log, appends the observed nonzero exit code, verifies every required sentinel and absence of collection errors, hashes/readbacks that immutable log before behavior implementation, and never commits an intentionally failing tree. Its green command uses the same Vitest argv with text-only 100% thresholds, writes only the separately owned green log, and requires exit zero. Verification reads/hash-checks green evidence and writes only its own verification log; no later command may open a red or prior green log for writing.

## Objective
Ship every accepted Clem feedback item end to end: correct shopping restoration, authenticated cross-device cook continuity, private saves, accepted manual tags, and backward-compatible API metadata. Preserve agentic-only import, current navigation, and neutral non-Pebble boundaries.

## Upstream Work Items
- `./2026-07-14-1313-clem-feedback-source.md` is the durable feedback source and item-by-item disposition.
- `./2026-07-14-1313-doing-clem-feedback-e2e/EXECUTION-CONTRACT.md` is the sole exact technical authority for schemas, CLI, storage, ordering, recovery, and terminal protocols; `UNIT-29.2-DETAIL.md` preserves detailed release requirements and maps them to Units 29.2.1-29.2.6.

## Completion Criteria
- [ ] Every line of the feedback source has an implemented or explicitly rejected disposition.
- [ ] Shopping re-add behavior matches the state matrix across web, REST v1, and MCP under repeated and concurrent calls.
- [ ] Workers-runtime tests prove deterministic user/recipe arbitration, first-writer/server-wins adoption, post-purge replay fencing, stale-delete isolation, SQLite DO persistence, attempt isolation, revision conflict/rebase, mutation dedupe, ordered alarms, purge barriers, private no-store responses, hibernation WebSockets, and the full Worker 101 response path.
- [ ] Two authenticated clients start/resume one session and synchronize step, checklist, and scale state; anonymous progress remains local-only.
- [ ] Recipe edits display pinned-state choices and never silently remap progress.
- [ ] My Kitchen cook/saved sections are owner-only for owner, authenticated visitor, and anonymous visitor cases.
- [ ] Completion and abandon clear resume state, preserve private history as intended, and create no RecipeSpoon/social side effect.
- [ ] SavedRecipe migration/backfill and all four cookbook membership writers obey the compatibility contract.
- [ ] Saved search is viewer-scoped without global-index leakage; private saved endpoints and entitled personalized `isSaved` projections are no-store, public-read-only bearer principals receive `isSaved: null` without private lookup, and only no-principal anonymous projections retain partitioned public caching.
- [ ] Manual course/custom tags author, filter, search, and project through REST and MCP recipe reads without any AI suggestion surface.
- [ ] REST v1 and MCP recipe-read additions pass compatibility, OpenAPI, contract, generator, tool-schema, list/detail/search/native-sync/write/cookbook, shared-math, and transport-parity tests.
- [ ] Current mobile dock remains stable; changed UI passes desktop/mobile visual QA with no overlap or unreachable controls.
- [ ] After production canonically contains the task merge SHA, either exactly or through a verified descendant, production visual dogfood covers every changed UI family on mobile/desktop plus the three guest-home viewports, with screenshot/live evidence, passing metrics, and a closed absurdity ledger before final cleanup.
- [ ] QA deploy, two-client smoke, purge, and residue inspection pass before merge.
- [ ] QA `/health` attests the exact PR head immediately before merge; the merge SHA's successful canonical CI push triggers the selected production `workflow_run`, whose artifact either promotes that exact source/tree/Worker version or proves it was safely superseded by a currently canonical descendant. Canonical `/health` attests the selected exact-or-descendant deployment before readiness/web/API smoke and cleanup pass.
- [ ] All tests and builds pass with zero warnings and 100% coverage on all new code, including `workers/**` and every task-owned executable script.
- [ ] Cleanup proves disposable relational/content-bearing state zero and separately records the exact retained identifier-bearing DO arbitration metadata; no evidence calls retained metadata product-data zero or physically erased.
- [ ] If UI/rendering/layout changed: `visual-qa-dogfood` evidence is captured, every absurdity ledger is closed, and automated visual metrics pass.
- [ ] After every product/Desk/archive/runtime terminal proof passes, reserve and attempt the exact Slugger handoff through the durable external notification journal. At most one process attempt may cross the immutable dispatch authorization boundary; contiguous paused attempts that are provably terminal/dead/reaped before authorization are replaced without effect. Observed zero/nonzero and crash-window uncertainty are reported truthfully, and no delivery/exactly-once claim is made after an authorized indeterminate dispatch.

- No coverage exclusions on new code.
- Cover every branch, auth/error response, null/empty input, numeric boundary, retry, conflict, race, and cleanup path.
- `workers/**` uses the real Cloudflare Workers Vitest project; app code uses the existing project.
- Focused script tests import and measure every touched executable. The exact BINARY-sorted pre-visual membership is `scripts/apply-reviewed-d1-migrations.ts`, `scripts/cleanup-local-qa-data.mjs`, `scripts/deploy-production.mjs`, `scripts/deployment-preflight.ts`, `scripts/feature-smoke-live.mjs`, `scripts/generate-api-playground.ts`, `scripts/production-readiness.ts`, `scripts/release-evidence-cli.ts`, `scripts/release-executor.ts`, `scripts/release-provider-command.mjs`, `scripts/release-spawn-gate.ts`, `scripts/release-terminal.ts`, `scripts/seed-qa.mjs`, `scripts/shopping-compat-catchup.mjs`, `scripts/smoke-api-live.mjs`, `scripts/smoke-live.mjs`, `scripts/smoke-mcp-oauth-live.mjs`, and `scripts/vite-build-sha.ts`. Unit30 compares exact ordered membership while preserving inherited entries. Unit31 compares the BINARY-sorted union with `scripts/production-visual-dogfood.mjs` as the exact nineteen-member final set and runs 100% coverage over it. Count-only agreement, substitution, omission, duplicate, or extra task-owned entry fails. Token-free pure `scripts/release-provenance.mjs`, pure `scripts/cloudflare-d1-query.mjs`, and changed executable root config `vite.config.ts` are additionally imported and measured under focused coverage; they are not part of the executable script-member count.
- Unit5's separate exact seed-entry registry is `prisma/seed.ts,scripts/seed-qa.mjs` and focused coverage measures both at 100%. Unit0.1 creates and measures pure non-executable `scripts/cloudflare-d1-query.mjs`, Unit5 consumes it for seed batching, and Unit29.1.2 extends its reviewed-migration use; Unit29.2 creates and measures pure non-executable `scripts/release-artifact-contract.mjs`. Full-suite coverage and script typecheck include both pure modules additively without counting either in executable membership.

## TDD Requirements
1. In each `a` unit, write every behavioral/error/coverage test named by the group and capture the expected red command/output as immutable task evidence, but do not commit or push an intentionally red tree.
2. In the matching `b` unit, implement without weakening the `a` tests, run green plus build/typecheck, then commit and push the tests and implementation together as the first checkpoint for that group.
3. The matching `c` unit is verification-only: run coverage/refactor/build commands and record evidence; do not add behavioral tests or implementation. If `c` finds a gap, reopen `a` with a new failing test, repeat `b`, then rerun `c`.
4. A group is complete only after `c` passes; update all three emojis/progress entries and run a fresh group review. For this task only, these four TDD requirements govern over generic Work Planner/Work Doer phase-commit and per-unit-status instructions: an `a` red tree is executed/evidenced but never committed or pushed; matching `a` tests and `b` implementation plus both status writes land together in one green atomic commit; `c` evidence and status land in their own verification commit. Test-first execution and every reviewer/verification gate remain mandatory.
5. Round111 makes the execution protocol uniform. Unit0.0 bootstraps and tests `scripts/tdd-evidence.mjs`; every later `a/b/c` triplet uses exact `pnpm tdd:evidence -- red|green|verify --manifest worker/tasks/2026-07-14-1313-doing-clem-feedback-e2e/tdd/unit-<id>.json`. The committed/hash-pinned manifest is required before `a`, and the execution contract freezes its schema, exact positive collection oracle, expected red failures/sentinels, text-only coverage set, warning classifier, write sets, and separate phase outputs. Any inline Vitest shell command below is only the manifest's inner-argv inventory; it is never an alternative evidence wrapper. A `c` unit never reruns or writes the `b` log.

If a competing product writer advances from the prepared predecessor while preserving the before doing bytes, persist cancelling plus the next `{remoteWinnerSha,localCandidateSha,convergenceSha}` to Desk before pushing convergenceSha, then consume cancelled through the exact no-content convergence, supersede, and restart from the winner. Recovery recognizes any already-pushed recorded convergenceSha; any changed doing bytes, unrecorded candidate, ninth race, or unclassifiable index/worktree/ref state fails closed. Every lifecycle checkpoint uses the shared Git matrix and candidate-byte journal.
**Output**: PR URL and `/Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2/clem-feedback-e2e/artifacts/release-<ReleaseRun.run>/unit-34/stage-<StageRun.run>/unit-34-evidence.json`.
**Acceptance**: PR head exactly equals the latest post-validating-transition Unit33 SHA; task/track are validating, product and Desk doing snapshots are byte-equal with exact PR line, transition journal is absent, TESTED_BASE_SHA is recorded/contained, and every finding has rerun Units32-34.

## Execution
- Placeholder glossary is authoritative for every vector below: `<M>` manifest, `<W>` writerId, `<R>` release run, `<U>` unit, `<G>` stage run, `<L>` logical name, `<A>` attempt, `<S>` SHA, `<K>` artifact kind, `<P>` artifact path, `<J>` canonical compact JSON including ProcessIdentity where required, `<N>` generation, `<PID>` process id, `<PGID>` process-group id, `<HOST>` executionHost, `<AGENT>` agent UUID, `<ROLE>` reviewer role, `<VERDICT>` verdict, and `<RUN_ATTEMPT>` positive workflow attempt. The old `<PSI>` free-form process-start identity is invalid.
- External Desk task is exact `/Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2/clem-feedback-e2e/task.md`; Units32-37 artifacts root is exact `/Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2/clem-feedback-e2e/artifacts/` until archive.
- Units32-37 use only the execution-contract-defined CLI for manifest/attempt transitions; ProcessCommand uses returned direct argv, while AgentCommand uses returned exact prompt bytes through the non-process sub-agent lifecycle. In the literal templates below `<M>` is the identity-owned absolute active or archived manifest path, `<I>` compact canonical ReleaseTaskIdentity JSON, `<W>` the init/recover writerId, `<R>` the current release run, `<U>` exact unit `32..37`, `<G>` its current stage run, `<L>` the next required logical name, `<A>` its attempt, `<S>` the required branch or merge SHA, `<K>` an exact artifact kind, `<P>` an absolute closed artifact path, and `<J>` one canonical compact JSON argv/evidence value; angle-bracket tokens are executor substitutions and never shell syntax. On first Unit32 use exact `pnpm release:evidence -- init --manifest <M> --identity-json <I>`; legacy `--task`/`--branch` init is invalid. When a manifest exists use exact `pnpm release:evidence -- recover --manifest <M> --writer-id <W>`. Then Unit32 alone runs exact `pnpm release:evidence -- start-run --manifest <M> --writer-id <W> --tested-base-sha <TESTED_BASE_SHA> --branch-head-sha <BRANCH_HEAD_SHA> --branch-head-tree-sha <BRANCH_HEAD_TREE_SHA>`. Every cwd, prompt, PR, continuation, Desk, worktree, archive, and receipt field derives from that persisted identity.
- The remaining exact mutating vectors are `start-stage --manifest <M> --writer-id <W> --release-run <R> --unit <U> --start-sha <S>`; `start-command --manifest <M> --writer-id <W> --release-run <R> --unit <U> --stage-run <G> --logical-name <L> --command-json <J>`; `prepare-spawn --manifest <M> --writer-id <W> --release-run <R> --unit <U> --stage-run <G> --logical-name <L> --attempt <A>`; `authorize-gate-spawn --manifest <M> --writer-id <W> --release-run <R> --unit <U> --stage-run <G> --logical-name <L> --attempt <A> --generation <N>`; ## Round 111 Ownership Override

Unit1.4 owns only the transitional shared web/REST service and preserves every current browser form. Unit15.2.1 atomically owns all final browser identity fields, persisted single-dispatch carriers, every current browser writer, receipt-status UI, CookStorageIdentity comparison, and strict server rejection. Unit1.0/0025 owns the final ShoppingMutationReceipt schema and all existing-source clock triggers; Unit18/0027 adds only SavedRecipe/membership-compatibility triggers and numeric ordering; Unit24/0028 adds only RecipeTag triggers. Unit0.0 owns the tested manifest evidence runner, and every later TDD triplet uses it with a committed harsh-reviewed manifest; inline shell commands are inner argv inventories only. Units29.1.2/29.1.5 own the permanent operation/attempt/singleton traffic-authority schema and direct pinned top-level production Wrangler deploy; Unit29.2.1 owns result/failure/archive parser parity and Unit29.2.2 owns its exact trusted direct child/environment/output policy. Unit37 accepts only independently reread D1, complete deployment percentages, referenced version lifecycle/binding/export, schedules, and health. The execution contract Round111 is sole byte/schema/protocol authority.

- 2026-07-17 Quality Round110's four clean-checkpoint lenses rejected convergence on fourteen deduplicated roots. Browser strict validation landed before its carrier; ten literal wrappers did not generalize to every triplet or positively prove collection/warnings; six verification units rewrote green ownership; Unit29.2.2b could edit its red gate; production used an undeclared Wrangler environment, wrong output variable, package-manager child, and a versions flow incapable of DO lifecycle/cron delivery; traffic predecessor scans were non-atomic; provider readback/failure schemas were incomplete; receipt retry scope/schema and 0025/0027/0028 trigger ownership were ambiguous. Round111 closes every root with the atomic Unit15.2.1 cutover, manifest runner, immutable phase artifacts, direct pinned top-level deploy, singleton D1 traffic CAS, complete official provider normalization, version-4 workflow evidence, exact receipt/window, and disjoint trigger registry. Fresh convergence starts after contract hash, commit, push, continuity, and Desk synchronization.
